## ğŸ§¬ WHAT ARE **PEPTIDES**?

**Peptides** are **short chains of amino acids**, usually 2â€“50 in length. Think of them as **mini proteins** â€” small enough to signal specific functions in your body **without triggering major side effects**.

They are like **biological text messages** your cells send each other to:
- heal tissue ğŸ©¹
- grow hair ğŸ’‡â€â™€ï¸
- burn fat ğŸ”¥
- boost focus ğŸ§ 
- regenerate nerves âš¡
- even improve sexual function ğŸ˜

## ğŸ§  PEPTIDES VS. PROTEINS

| Property       | Peptides                          | Proteins                     |
|----------------|-----------------------------------|------------------------------|
| Size           | Tiny (2â€“50 amino acids)           | Big (>50 amino acids)        |
| Function       | Specific signals (e.g., repair)   | Structural (muscles, enzymes)|
| Absorption     | Often injectable or nasal         | Broken down in digestion     |
